\hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension}{}\doxysection{scifir\+::dimension Class Reference}
\label{classscifir_1_1dimension}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}


Class that represents dimensions of the SI system of units. Each prefix sizes 6 bytes, 1 byte for the dimension type, 1 byte for the prefix, 1 byte for the position (which can be the NUMERATOR or the DENOMINATOR), and 3 bytes for the custom dimension (in case it\textquotesingle{}s used one).  




{\ttfamily \#include $<$dimension.\+hpp$>$}

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Represents a dimension of the SI system of units. All the dimensions of the SI system of units are supported. There are also dimensions supported that aren\textquotesingle{}t considered yet part of the SI system of units, but that are widely used. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42a}{position}} \+: int8\+\_\+t \{ \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa606caf7befec312f8221bc2d191071c2}{NO\+\_\+\+POSITION}}
, \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aaca5d501f305756a8271b1c629bb2f41c}{NUMERATOR}}
, \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa10c8649258e57040c30a4f639eca7717}{DENOMINATOR}}
 \}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Represents the position of the dimension, which can be at the numerator or at the denominator. The value NO\+\_\+\+POSITION is used when there\textquotesingle{}s no position specified. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Class that represents dimensions of the SI system of units. Each prefix sizes 6 bytes, 1 byte for the dimension type, 1 byte for the prefix, 1 byte for the position (which can be the NUMERATOR or the DENOMINATOR), and 3 bytes for the custom dimension (in case it\textquotesingle{}s used one). 

Definition at line 28 of file dimension.\+hpp.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{position}{position}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42a}{scifir\+::dimension\+::position}} \+: int8\+\_\+t}



Represents the position of the dimension, which can be at the numerator or at the denominator. The value NO\+\_\+\+POSITION is used when there\textquotesingle{}s no position specified. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{NO\_POSITION@{NO\_POSITION}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!NO\_POSITION@{NO\_POSITION}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa606caf7befec312f8221bc2d191071c2}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa606caf7befec312f8221bc2d191071c2}} 
NO\+\_\+\+POSITION&The dimension is not ready and yet being used. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{NUMERATOR@{NUMERATOR}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!NUMERATOR@{NUMERATOR}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aaca5d501f305756a8271b1c629bb2f41c}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aaca5d501f305756a8271b1c629bb2f41c}} 
NUMERATOR&The dimension is at the numerator. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{DENOMINATOR@{DENOMINATOR}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!DENOMINATOR@{DENOMINATOR}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa10c8649258e57040c30a4f639eca7717}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42aa10c8649258e57040c30a4f639eca7717}} 
DENOMINATOR&The dimension is at the denominator. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fb}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fb}} 
\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!type@{type}}
\index{type@{type}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{type}{type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fb}{scifir\+::dimension\+::type}} \+: int8\+\_\+t}



Represents a dimension of the SI system of units. All the dimensions of the SI system of units are supported. There are also dimensions supported that aren\textquotesingle{}t considered yet part of the SI system of units, but that are widely used.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{ASTRONOMICAL\_UNIT@{ASTRONOMICAL\_UNIT}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!ASTRONOMICAL\_UNIT@{ASTRONOMICAL\_UNIT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba6b41c70a280cb0a02b1654fafff3dc1e}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba6b41c70a280cb0a02b1654fafff3dc1e}} 
ASTRONOMICAL\+\_\+\+UNIT&Astronomical Unit. Dimension of length. Defined as the distance from the Sun to the Earth. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{PARSEC@{PARSEC}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!PARSEC@{PARSEC}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fbae46e31f2a196a326dd1a7f423147cb6d}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fbae46e31f2a196a326dd1a7f423147cb6d}} 
PARSEC&Parsec. Dimension of length. Defined as the distance where 1 AU subtends an angle of 1 second of arc. Equivalent to 3.\+26156 light years. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{ELECTRON\_VOLT@{ELECTRON\_VOLT}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!ELECTRON\_VOLT@{ELECTRON\_VOLT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba43e32b0961d06ad1f66903833f7c8c3b}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba43e32b0961d06ad1f66903833f7c8c3b}} 
ELECTRON\+\_\+\+VOLT&Electron volt. Dimension of energy. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{DALTON@{DALTON}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!DALTON@{DALTON}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba50f18d4f59c9202a0826217327fea8fc}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba50f18d4f59c9202a0826217327fea8fc}} 
DALTON&Dalton. Dimension of mass. Used to measure the mass of atoms and molecules. Defined as 1/12 of a C-\/12. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{ATOMIC\_MASS\_UNIT@{ATOMIC\_MASS\_UNIT}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!ATOMIC\_MASS\_UNIT@{ATOMIC\_MASS\_UNIT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba67da7e36029ed662fd6e717735561492}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba67da7e36029ed662fd6e717735561492}} 
ATOMIC\+\_\+\+MASS\+\_\+\+UNIT&Atomic mass unit. Equivalent to the Dalton. Dimension of mass. Used to measure the mass of atoms and molecules. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{BARN@{BARN}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!BARN@{BARN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba2ef28355046604f1fcfb9bdd8284e620}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba2ef28355046604f1fcfb9bdd8284e620}} 
BARN&Barn. Dimension of area. It\textquotesingle{}s used inside nuclear physics to express the transversal section of nucleus and nuclear reactions. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MOLARITY@{MOLARITY}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!MOLARITY@{MOLARITY}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba0ac4f9fa9723f528a6e9ef07a8f51507}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba0ac4f9fa9723f528a6e9ef07a8f51507}} 
MOLARITY&Molarity. Dimension of concentration of a chemical species. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{PARTICLES@{PARTICLES}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!PARTICLES@{PARTICLES}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba8ea708047a9699f9b4570b07a6135a3e}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fba8ea708047a9699f9b4570b07a6135a3e}} 
PARTICLES&Particles. It\textquotesingle{}s not exactly a dimension, it corresponds to the brute amount of particles, as opposed to the mole. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CUSTOM@{CUSTOM}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!CUSTOM@{CUSTOM}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fbafd6586f52e600f9ba2e7c4ba597a2ce1}\label{classscifir_1_1dimension_a7159ee72510ebcc26ee93da8900fb9fbafd6586f52e600f9ba2e7c4ba597a2ce1}} 
CUSTOM&Custom dimension. It means the dimension is a custom dimension, which can have any value and meaning, defined freely by the programmer. Each custom dimension is unique to where it\textquotesingle{}s defined and used. \\

MONEY&Money. The money is not specified in a specific currency, you must use the ISO 4217 of currencies for that purpose. Don\textquotesingle{}t mistake mixing different currencies. \\

PIXEL&Amount of pixels. Used for screen sizes. It can also be used as distance, in replacement of length dimensions, if in a virtual space it\textquotesingle{}s thinked in pixels instead of normal dimensions of length. \\

MEMO&Invented unit inside Scifir, it\textquotesingle{}s not part of the SI system of units. It represents a unit of human or animal memory. Each memory of the brain has some size hypothetically measurable in memos. \\

\index{scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}!prefix\_math@{prefix\_math}}
\index{prefix\_math@{prefix\_math}!scifir::dimension@{scifir::dimension}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{prefix\_math()}{prefix\_math()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily long double dimension\+::prefix\+\_\+math (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Returns the math between the prefix and the dimension, which varies if the dimension is a B or another. In the case of bytes the math with the prefix is different, it\textquotesingle{}s done with 1024 instead of multiples of 10. It doesn\textquotesingle{}t includes the conversion factor of dimensions.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension_a0c5cc98c4cc5074dc6d68b9d36aff42a}{dimension\+::position}} dimension\+::dimension\+\_\+position}



The position of the dimension, which can be the NUMERATOR, the DENOMINATOR or NO\+\_\+\+POSITION. NO\+\_\+\+POSITION means that the dimension is not ready to be used, and must be changed if the dimension is intended to be used.
